<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Certain Relationships and Related Party Transactions </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Investment Management Agreement </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company is party to an investment management agreement, pursuant to which the Company pays GSAM, a wholly owned subsidiary of Group Inc., a
fee for investment management services consisting of a management fee based on the Company&#146;s gross assets (excluding cash and cash equivalents but including assets purchased with borrowed amounts) and an incentive fee based on the performance
of the Company&#146;s investments. Certain of the Company&#146;s officers are also officers and employees of GSAM. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the year ended
December&nbsp;31, 2021, the management fee was calculated at an annual rate of 1.00% (0.25% per quarter) of the average value of the Company&#146;s gross assets at the end of each of the two most recently completed calendar quarters, and the
incentive fee was calculated based on (a)&nbsp;the amount by which our ordinary income exceeds certain &#147;hurdle rates,&#148; and (b)&nbsp;our capital gains. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2021, the Company paid GSAM a total of $41.21&nbsp;million in fees (excluding fees that are accrued but
not paid) pursuant to the investment management agreement, which consisted of $29.69&nbsp;million in management fees and $11.52&nbsp;million in incentive fees. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">18 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>License Agreement </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company is party to a license agreement with an affiliate of Goldman Sachs pursuant to which the Company has been granted a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-exclusive,</FONT> royalty-free license to use the &#147;Goldman Sachs&#148; name. Under this agreement, the Company does not have a right to use the Goldman Sachs name if GSAM or another affiliate of Goldman Sachs is
not the Company&#146;s investment adviser or if the Company&#146;s continued use of such license results in a violation of applicable law, results in a regulatory burden or has adverse regulatory consequences. Other than with respect to this limited
license, the Company has no legal right to the &#147;Goldman Sachs&#148; name. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Investment</FONT> Opportunities
</I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company has in the past <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-invested,</FONT> and in the future may <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-invest,</FONT> on a concurrent basis with other funds managed by GSAM and its affiliates, but not if such <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-investment</FONT> is impermissible under existing regulatory guidance,
applicable regulations or GSAM&#146;s allocation procedures. Certain types of negotiated <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-investments</FONT> may be made only if the Company receives an order from the SEC permitting the Company to do so. On
January 4, 2017, the SEC granted to GSAM and the BDCs advised by GSAM exemptive relief to co-invest with other funds managed by GSAM in a manner consistent with our investment objectives, positions, policies, strategies and restrictions as well as
regulatory requirements and other pertinent factors (the &#147;Relief&#148;). Additionally, if GSAM forms certain other client accounts managed by GSAM in the future, we may co-invest on a concurrent basis with such other affiliates, subject to
compliance with the Relief, applicable regulations and regulatory guidance, as well as applicable allocation procedures. On March 15, 2022, the SEC published a notice of an application that is intended to supersede the Relief and, if granted, would
permit limited additional flexibility for the Company to enter into co-investment transactions with proprietary accounts of The Goldman Sachs Group, Inc., its subsidiaries and its affiliates. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Related Party Transaction Review Policy </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit Committee will review any potential related party transactions brought to its attention, and, during these reviews, will consider any
conflicts of interest brought to its attention pursuant to the Company&#146;s Code of Ethics. Each of the Company&#146;s directors and executive officers is instructed and periodically reminded to inform GSAM Compliance of any potential related
party transactions. In addition, each such director and executive officer completes a questionnaire on an annual basis designed to elicit information about any potential related party transactions. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">19 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>PROPOSAL 2 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>RATIFICATION OF SELECTION OF INDEPENDENT REGISTERED PUBLIC ACCOUNTING FIRM </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">At a meeting of the Board held on December&nbsp;7, 2021, the Audit Committee selected and recommended, and the Board, including a majority of
the Independent Directors approved, the selection of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP to act as the independent registered public accounting firm for the Company for the fiscal year ending December&nbsp;31, 2022. This selection is presented for
ratification by the Stockholders. If the Stockholders fail to ratify the selection of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP to serve as the independent registered public accounting firm for the year ending December&nbsp;31, 2022, the Audit Committee and the
Board will reconsider the continued retention of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Representatives of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP are expected
to be available telephonically during the Meeting and will be available to respond to appropriate questions from Stockholders if necessary. Representatives of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP will be given the opportunity to make statements at the
Meeting, if they so desire. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Audit Fees </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The aggregate audit fees billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2021 and 2020 were $894,017 and $987,750,
respectively. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fees included in the audit fees category are those associated with the annual audits of financial statements, review of the
financial statements included in the Company&#146;s Quarterly Reports on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Form&nbsp;10-Q&nbsp;and</FONT> services that are normally provided in connection with statutory and regulatory filings. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Audit-Related Fees </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The aggregate
audit-related fees billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2021 and 2020 were $0 and $697,000, respectively. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Audit-related fees are for any services rendered to the Company that are reasonably related to the performance of the audits or reviews of the
Company&#146;s consolidated financial statements (but not reported as audit fees above). These services include attestation services that are not required by statute or regulation and consultations concerning financial accounting and reporting
standards. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The aggregate audit-related fees billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP to GSAM, and any entity controlling, controlled by, or
under common control with, GSAM, that provides ongoing services to the Company, for engagements directly related to the Company&#146;s operations and financial reporting, for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2021 and 2020 were $1,116,432 and
$1,126,432, respectively. These amounts represent fees PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP billed to GSAM for services related to the SSAE 18 report. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Tax
Fees </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">No fees were billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for services rendered to the Company for tax compliance, tax advice and tax
planning for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2021 and 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fees included in the tax fees category comprise all services performed by
professional staff in the independent registered public accountant&#146;s tax division except those services related to the audits. This category comprises fees for tax compliance services provided in connection with the preparation and review of
the Company&#146;s tax returns. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">20 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">No tax fees were billed by the Company&#146;s independent registered public accountant to GSAM,
and any entity controlling, controlled by, or under common control with, GSAM, that provides ongoing services to the Company, for engagements directly related to the Company&#146;s operations and financial reporting, for the years ended
December&nbsp;31, 2021 and 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>All Other Fees </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">No fees were billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for products and services provided to the Company, other than the services reported in
&#147;Audit Fees&#148; and &#147;Tax Fees&#148; above, for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2021 and 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Other than services reported
under &#147;Audit-Related Fees,&#148; no other fees were billed by the Company&#146;s independent registered public accountant to GSAM, and any entity controlling, controlled by, or under common control with, GSAM, that provides ongoing services to
the Company, for engagements directly related to the Company&#146;s operations and financial reporting, for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2021 and 2020. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Aggregate&nbsp;Non-Audit&nbsp;Fees</FONT> </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">No <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> fees were billed to the Company&#146;s investment adviser and service affiliates by
PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2021 and 2020. This includes any <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services required to be <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approved</FONT> or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services that did not require <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval</FONT> since they did not directly relate to the Company&#146;s
operations or financial reporting. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Pre-Approval</FONT> of Audit and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Audit</FONT>
Services Provided to the Company </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">and&nbsp;Non-Audit&nbsp;Services&nbsp;Pre-Approval&nbsp;Policy</FONT></FONT> (the &#147;Policy&#148;) adopted by the Audit Committee sets forth the procedures and the conditions
pursuant to which services performed by an independent auditor for the Company may <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">be&nbsp;pre-approved.&nbsp;Services</FONT> may <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">be&nbsp;pre-approved&nbsp;specifically</FONT> by the
Audit Committee as a whole or, in certain circumstances, by the Audit Committee Chairman or the person designated as the audit committee financial expert. In addition, subject to specified cost limitations, certain services may <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">be&nbsp;pre-approved&nbsp;under</FONT> the provisions of the Policy. The Policy provides that the Audit Committee will consider whether the services provided by an independent auditor are consistent with the SEC&#146;s
rules on auditor independence. The Policy provides for periodic review <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">and&nbsp;pre-approval&nbsp;by</FONT> the Audit Committee of the services that may be provided by the independent auditor. All of the audit and
permitted <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services described above for which PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP billed the Company for the fiscal years ended December&nbsp;31, 2021 and 2020 were
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approved</FONT> by the Audit Committee. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>De Minimis Waiver</I>.
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">The&nbsp;pre-approval&nbsp;requirements</FONT> of the Policy may be waived with respect to the provision <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-audit&nbsp;services</FONT> that are permissible for an independent
auditor to perform, provided (1)&nbsp;the aggregate amount of all such services provided constitutes no more than five percent of the total amount of revenues subject <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">to&nbsp;pre-approval&nbsp;that</FONT> was paid to
the independent auditors during the fiscal year in which the services are provided; (2)&nbsp;such services were not recognized by the Company at the time of the engagement to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">be&nbsp;non-audit&nbsp;services;</FONT>
and (3)&nbsp;such services are promptly brought to the attention of the Audit Committee and approved prior to the completion of the audit by the Audit Committee or by one or more members of the Audit Committee to whom authority to grant such
approvals has been delegated by the Audit Committee, pursuant to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;pre-approval&nbsp;provisions</FONT> of the Policy. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Pre-Approval</FONT></I><I></I><I>&nbsp;of</I><I></I><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&nbsp;
Non-Audit</FONT></I><I></I><I>&nbsp;Services Provided to GSAM.</I>&nbsp;The Policy provides that, in addition to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">requiring&nbsp;pre-approval&nbsp;of</FONT> audit
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">and&nbsp;non-audit&nbsp;services</FONT> provided to the Company, the Audit Committee
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">will&nbsp;pre-approve&nbsp;those&nbsp;non-audit&nbsp;services</FONT></FONT> provided to the Company&#146;s investment adviser (and entities controlling, controlled by or under common
control with the investment adviser that provide ongoing services to the Company) where the engagement relates directly to the operations or financial reporting of the Company. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">21 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit Committee has considered these fees and the nature of the services rendered and has
concluded that they are compatible with maintaining the independence of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP. The Audit Committee did not approve any of the audit-related, tax, or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">other&nbsp;non-audit&nbsp;fees</FONT>
described above pursuant to the &#147;<I>de minimis</I>&nbsp;exceptions&#148; set forth in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Rule&nbsp;2-01(c)(7)(i)(C)&nbsp;and</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Rule&nbsp;2-01(c)(7)(ii)&nbsp;of</FONT> <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Regulation&nbsp;S-X.&nbsp;Except</FONT> as described above, PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP did not provide any audit-related services, tax services or other non-audit&nbsp;services to GSAM or any entity controlling, controlled
by or under common control with GSAM that provides ongoing services to the Company that the Audit Committee was required to approve pursuant to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Rule&nbsp;2-01(c)(7)(ii)&nbsp;of</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Regulation&nbsp;S-X.&nbsp;The</FONT> Audit Committee considered whether the provision of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services rendered to GSAM and any entity controlling, controlled by, or under
common control with GSAM that provides ongoing services to the Company that were <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">not&nbsp;pre-approved&nbsp;by</FONT> the Audit Committee because the engagement did not relate directly to the operations and financial
reporting of the Company is compatible with maintaining PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP&#146;s independence. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ON MARCH&nbsp;2, 2022, THE
BOARD, INCLUDING EACH OF THE INDEPENDENT DIRECTORS, UNANIMOUSLY RECOMMENDED THAT YOU VOTE &#147;FOR&#148; THE RATIFICATION OF PRICEWATERHOUSECOOPERS LLP AS INDEPENDENT REGISTERED PUBLIC ACCOUNTING FIRM TO THE COMPANY FOR THE FISCAL YEAR ENDING
DECEMBER&nbsp;31, 2022. </B></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">22 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><I>Audit Committee Report <SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">(1)</SUP> </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following is the report of the Audit Committee of Goldman Sachs BDC, Inc. (the &#147;Company&#148;) with respect to the Company&#146;s
audited financial statements for the fiscal year ended December&nbsp;31, 2021 (the &#147;Audited Financial Statements&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit
Committee has: (a)&nbsp;reviewed and discussed the Audited Financial Statements with the management of the Company; (b)&nbsp;discussed with the independent auditor the matters required to be discussed by Auditing Standard 1301 (Communications with
Audit Committees), as adopted by the Public Company Accounting Oversight Board (&#147;PCAOB&#148;); and (c)&nbsp;received the written disclosures and the letter from the independent auditor required by applicable requirements of the PCAOB Ethics and
Independence Rule 3526 regarding the independent auditor&#146;s communications with the Audit Committee concerning independence, and has discussed with the independent auditor the auditor&#146;s independence. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The members of the Audit Committee are not, and do not represent themselves to be, professionally engaged in the practice of auditing or
accounting and are not employed by the Company for accounting, financial management or internal control purposes. Moreover, the Audit Committee relies on and makes no independent verification of the facts presented to it or representations made by
management or the Company&#146;s independent auditor. Accordingly, the Audit Committee&#146;s oversight does not provide an independent basis to determine that management has maintained appropriate accounting and/or financial reporting principles
and policies, or internal controls and procedures designed to assure compliance with accounting standards and applicable laws and regulations. Furthermore, the Audit Committee&#146;s considerations and discussions referred to above do not provide
assurance that the audit of the Company&#146;s financial statements has been carried out in accordance with the standards of the PCAOB or that the financial statements are presented in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Based on its consideration of the Audited Financial Statements and the discussions referred to above with management and the Company&#146;s
independent auditor, and subject to the limitations on the responsibilities and role of the Audit Committee set forth in the charter and those discussed above, the Audit Committee recommended to the Board of Directors that the Audited Financial
Statements be accepted by the Board of Directors and included in the Company&#146;s Annual Report on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-K</FONT> for the last fiscal year for filing with the SEC. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">March&nbsp;2, 2022 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>The Audit
Committee </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Richard A. Mark, Chairman </P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>OTHER BUSINESS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The management of the Company does not know of any other matters to be brought before the Meeting. If such matters are properly brought before
the Meeting, proxies that do not contain specific instructions to the contrary will be voted in accordance with the judgment of Caroline Kraus and Lindsey Edwards, who are the persons named as proxies. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>VOTE REQUIRED FOR THE ELECTION OF THE DIRECTOR AND </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>APPROVAL OF OTHER MATTERS AT THE MEETING </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A quorum for the transaction of business at the Meeting is established by the presence, virtually or by proxy, of holders representing a
majority of the votes entitled to be cast at the Meeting. Stockholders of record at the close of business on the Record Date are entitled to receive notice of, and to vote at, the Meeting and at any postponements or adjournments thereof. There were
101,885,413 shares of the Company&#146;s common stock outstanding on April&nbsp;1, 2022. Each share of common stock is entitled to one vote. Cumulative voting is not permitted. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Election of Directors </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For Proposal 1,
the election of each nominee requires a majority of the votes cast by all Stockholders present, virtually or by proxy, at the Meeting, provided that if, as of the tenth (10th) day preceding the date the Company first mails the notice of such meeting
to the Stockholders, the number of nominees for the directorships (or, if applicable, the directorships of a particular class of directors) exceeds the number of such directors to be elected, such directors shall be elected by the vote of a
plurality of the votes cast. Under the Company&#146;s bylaws, a majority of votes cast means that the number of votes cast &#147;for&#148; a director&#146;s election exceeds the number of votes cast &#147;against&#148; that director&#146;s election
(with &#147;abstentions&#148; and &#147;broker <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-votes&#148;</FONT> not counted as a vote cast either &#147;for&#148; or &#147;against&#148; that director&#146;s election). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Ratification of Auditor </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Approval of
Proposal 2, the ratification of the selection of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP to serve as the Company&#146;s independent registered public accounting firm, requires a majority of the votes by all Stockholders present, virtually or by proxy, at the
Meeting. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Broker <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Votes</FONT> </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Broker <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;non-votes&#148;</FONT> are shares held in an account with an Authorized Institution for which the
broker indicates that instructions have not been received from the beneficial owners or other persons entitled to vote, and the broker does not have discretionary voting authority with respect to a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-routine</FONT>
proposal. As broker <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-votes</FONT> are entitled to vote on Proposal 2, broker <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-votes</FONT> will be counted as shares present for purposes of determining whether a quorum is
present for purposes of transacting business at the Meeting. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Proposal 1 is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-routine</FONT> matter.
As a result, if you hold shares in &#147;street name&#148; through a broker, bank or other nominee, your broker, bank or nominee will <B>not </B>be permitted to exercise voting discretion with respect to Proposal 1, the election of three
Class&nbsp;II directors. Therefore, if you do not vote and you do not give your broker or other nominee specific instructions on how to vote for you, then your shares will have no effect on Proposal 1. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Proposal 2, the ratification of the selection of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP to serve as the Company&#146;s independent registered public
accounting firm, is a routine matter. As a result, if you beneficially own your shares and you do not provide your broker or nominee with voting instructions, then your broker, bank or nominee will be able to vote your shares for you on Proposal 2.
</P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">24 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Abstentions </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Abstentions will be counted as shares present for purposes of determining whether a quorum is present, but will not be voted for or against the
Proposal for which the proxy card has been marked &#147;Abstain&#148;. Accordingly, abstentions will have no effect on Proposal 1, and the effect of a vote against Proposal 2. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Adjournment </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If less than a quorum is
present at the Meeting or if an insufficient number of votes is present for the approval of the Proposals, the chairman of the Meeting shall have the power to adjourn the Meeting from time to time without notice other than announcement at the
Meeting. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A vote may be taken on either Proposal prior to any such adjournment if there are sufficient votes for approval of such
Proposal. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>COMMUNICATIONS WITH THE BOARD </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">All interested parties, including Stockholders, may send communications to the Board, the Independent Directors, the Chairman or any other
individual director, by addressing such communication to the Board, the Independent Directors, the Chairman or to the individual director, c/o Goldman Sachs Asset Management, L.P., 200 West Street, New York, New York 10282. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ANNUAL AND QUARTERLY REPORTS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Copies of the Company&#146;s Annual Reports on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-K,</FONT> Quarterly Reports on Form <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-Q</FONT> and Current Reports on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">8-K</FONT> are available, without charge, on its website (<I><U>https://www.goldmansachsbdc.com</U></I>)<I> </I>or upon request by writing to the
Company or by calling the Company toll-free at (866) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">904-6150.</FONT> Please direct your written request to Caroline Kraus, Secretary, at the Company, c/o Goldman Sachs Asset Management, L.P., 200 West Street, New
York, New York 10282. Copies of such reports are also posted and are available without charge on the SEC&#146;s website at <I><U>www.sec.gov</U></I>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>CORPORATE GOVERNANCE </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Code of Ethics
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company has adopted a Code of Ethics pursuant to Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">17j-1</FONT> under the 1940 Act and the
Company has also approved GSAM&#146;s Code of Ethics that it adopted in accordance with Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">17j-1</FONT> and Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">204A-1</FONT> under the Investment Advisers Act of 1940, as amended.
These Codes of Ethics establish, among other things, procedures for personal investments and restrict certain personal securities transactions, including transactions in securities that are held by the Company. Personnel subject to each code may
invest in securities for their personal investment accounts, so long as such investments are made in accordance with the code&#146;s requirements. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Code of Business Conduct and Ethics </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The
Company has adopted a Code of Business Conduct and Ethics which applies to, among others, the Company&#146;s Chief Executive Officer and Chief Financial Officer. The Company intends to disclose any material amendment to or waivers of required
provisions of the Code of Business Conduct and Ethics on a current report on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">8-K</FONT> or on the Company&#146;s website. The Code of Business Conduct and Ethics can be accessed via the Company&#146;s website
(<I><U>https://www.goldmansachsbdc.com</U></I>). </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Corporate Governance Guidelines and Director Charter </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company has adopted a Corporate Governance Guidelines and Director Charter which applies to, among other things, the authority and duties
of the directors, the composition of the Board and the election and role of the Chairman of the Board. The Corporate Governance Guidelines and Director Charter can be accessed via the Company&#146;s website
(<I><U>https://www.goldmansachsbdc.com</U></I>). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ADDITIONAL INFORMATION </B></P>
